          # Returns number of bytes of the specified data type

          1
          
          def size_of(val)
        
      2250. 
      
        
    2250. 
          3
          
             case val 
        
      2251. 
      
        
    2251. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'long' )
        
      2252. 
      
        
    2252. 
          
          
                return(4)
        
      2253. 
      
        
    2253. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'longlong' )
        
      2254. 
      
        
    2254. 
          
          
                return(8)
        
      2255. 
      
        
    2255. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'char' )
        
      2256. 
      
        
    2256. 
          
          
                return(1)
        
      2257. 
      
        
    2257. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'double' )
        
      2258. 
      
        
    2258. 
          
          
                return(8)
        
      2259. 
      
        
    2259. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'float' )
        
      2260. 
      
        
    2260. 
          
          
                return(4)
        
      2261. 
      
        
    2261. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'int' )
        
      2262. 
      
        
    2262. 
          
          
                return(4)
        
      2263. 
      
        
    2263. 
          3
          
             when (val == 'short' )
        
      2264. 
      
        
    2264. 
          
          
                return(2)
        
      2265. 
      
        
    2265. 
          
          
             else
        
      2266. 
      
        
    2266. 
          3
          
                return(1)
        
      2267. 
      
        
    2267. 
          
          
             end
        
      2268. 
      
        
    2268. 
          
          
          end

          # Error report gets displayed on screen. If the parameter is omitted, will report
        
      2272. 
      
        
    2272. 
          
          
          # a Syntax Error and cite the offending line. Otherwise, the text given in the

    2273.

      2274.

          1
          
          def error_report(text="")
        
      2276. 
      
        
    2276. 
          
          
            if text.eql?""
        
      2277. 
      
        
    2277. 
          
          
              puts "Syntax Error: \"#{@@inputarr[@@line_number-1]}\""
        
      2278. 
      
        
    2278. 
          
          
              #if @@options.debug
        
      2279. 
      
        
    2279. 
          
          
                write_error_report_to_file "Syntax Error: \"#{@@inputarr[@@line_number-1]}\""
        
      2280. 
      
        
    2280. 
          
          
              #end
        
      2281. 
      
        
    2281. 
          
          
            else
        
      2282. 
      
        
    2282. 
          
          
              puts "#{text}"
        
      2283. 
      
        
    2283. 
          
          
              #if @@options.debug
        
      2284. 
      
        
    2284. 
          
          
                write_error_report_to_file "#{text}"
        
      2285. 
      
        
    2285. 
          
          
              #end
        
      2286. 
      
        
    2286. 
          
          
            end
        
      2287. 
      
        
    2287. 
          
          
          end

      51. 
      
        
    51. 
          
          
                     debug_files.zip will be created, containing input files
        
      52. 
      
        
    52. 
          
          
                     and intermediate files generated during the parsing process.
        
      53. 
      
        
    53. 
          
          
                     
        
      54. 
      
        
    54. 
          1
          
          END_OF_SYNTAX
        
      55. 
      
        
    55. 
          1
          
              exit
        
      56. 
      
        
    56. 
          
          
            end
        
      57. 
      
        
    57. 
          
          
          
        
      58. 
      
        
    58. 
          
          
          end

          1
          
          class ParseCommandLine
        
      66. 
      
        
    66. 
          
          
          
        
      67. 
      
        
    67. 
          1
          
            def self.parse(argv)
        
      68. 
      
        
    68. 
          1
          
              options = OpenStruct.new
        
      69. 
      
        
    69. 
          
          
          
        
      70. 
      
        
    70. 
          1
          
              options.args = argv.clone
        
      71. 
      
        
    71. 
          1
          
              options.cpp = ""
        
      72. 
      
        
    72. 
          1
          
              options.include_paths = []
        
      73. 
      
        
    73. 
          1
          
              options.include_files = []
        
      74. 
      
        
    74. 
          1
          
              options.header_files = []
        
      75. 
      
        
    75. 
          1
          
              options.macros = []
        
      76. 
      
        
    76. 
          1
          
              options.outfile = ""
        
      77. 
      
        
    77. 
          1
          
              options.directory = Dir.pwd
        
      78. 
      
        
    78. 
          1
          
              options.help = false
        
      79. 
      
        
    79. 
          1
          
              options.verbose = false
        
      80. 
      
        
    80. 
          1
          
              options.debug = false
        
      81. 
      
        
    81. 
          
          
          
        
      82. 
      
        
    82. 
          1
          
              opts = OptionParser.new do |opts|
        
      83. 
      
        
    83. 
          
          
          
        
      84. 
      
        
    84. 
          1
          
                opts.on("--cpp S", String) do |s|
        
      85. 
      
        
    85. 
          
          
                  options.cpp = s
        
      86. 
      
        
    86. 
          
          
                  if s =~ /\s/
        
      87. 
      
        
    87. 
          
          
                    ind = options.args.index(s)
        
      88. 
      
        
    88. 
          
          
                    options.args[ind] = "'" + options.args[ind] + "'"
        
      89. 
      
        
    89. 
          
          
                  end
        
      90. 
      
        
    90. 
          
          
                end
        
      91. 
      
        
    91. 
          
          
          
        
      92. 
      
        
    92. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-I S", String) do |s|
        
      93. 
      
        
    93. 
          1
          
                  dirarr = s.split
        
      94. 
      
        
    94. 
          2
          
                  dirarr.each {|d| options.include_paths.insert(-1, d)}
        
      95. 
      
        
    95. 
          
          
                end
        
      96. 
      
        
    96. 
          
          
          
        
      97. 
      
        
    97. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-i S", String) do |s|
        
      98. 
      
        
    98. 
          1
          
                  filarr = s.split
        
      99. 
      
        
    99. 
          2
          
                  filarr.each {|f| options.include_files.insert(-1, f)}
        
      100. 
      
        
    100. 
          
          
                end
        
      101. 
      
        
    101. 
          
          
          
        
      102. 
      
        
    102. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-D M", String) do |m|
        
      103. 
      
        
    103. 
          1
          
                  options.macros.insert(-1, m)
        
      104. 
      
        
    104. 
          
          
                end
        
      105. 
      
        
    105. 
          
          
          
        
      106. 
      
        
    106. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-o S", String) do |s|
        
      107. 
      
        
    107. 
          1
          
                  options.outfile = s
        
      108. 
      
        
    108. 
          
          
                end
        
      109. 
      
        
    109. 
          
          
          
        
      110. 
      
        
    110. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-h", "--help") do
        
      111. 
      
        
    111. 
          1
          
                  options.help = true
        
      112. 
      
        
    112. 
          
          
                end
        
      113. 
      
        
    113. 
          
          
          
        
      114. 
      
        
    114. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-v", "--verbose") do
        
      115. 
      
        
    115. 
          1
          
                  options.verbose = true
        
      116. 
      
        
    116. 
          
          
                end
        
      117. 
      
        
    117. 
          
          
          
        
      118. 
      
        
    118. 
          1
          
                opts.on("-d", "--debug") do
        
      119. 
      
        
    119. 
          1
          
                  options.debug = true
        
      120. 
      
        
    120. 
          
          
                end
        
      121. 
      
        
    121. 
          
          
          
        
      122. 
      
        
    122. 
          
          
              end
        
      123. 
      
        
    123. 
          
          
          
        
      124. 
      
        
    124. 
          1
          
              options.header_files = opts.parse!(argv)
        
      125. 
      
        
    125. 
          2
          
              options.header_files.collect!{|f| File.expand_path(f)}
        
      126. 
      
        
    126. 
          1
          
              options
        
      127. 
      
        
    127. 
          
          
            end
        
      128. 
      
        
    128. 
          
          
          
        
      129. 
      
        
    129. 
          
          
          end
        
      130.

      131. 
      
        
    131. 
          
          
          #
        
      132. 
      
        
    132. 
          
          
          # Performs a check of user provided arguments 
        
      133. 
      
        
    133. 
          
          
          #
        
      134. 
      
        
    134. 
          1
          
          class ArgumentCheck
        
      135. 
      
        
    135. 
          
          
          
        
      136. 
      
        
    136. 
          1
          
            def self.check
        
      137. 
      
        
    137. 
          2
          
              SyntaxDescription.describe() if @@options.help == true
        
      138. 
      
        
    138. 
          
          
          
        
      139. 
      
        
    139. 
          
          
              # Check cpp
        
      140. 
      
        
    140. 
          2
          
              if not @@options.cpp.empty?
        
      141. 
      
        
    141. 
          1
          
                file = @@options.cpp.split[0]
        
      142. 
      
        
    142. 
          1
          
                raise ArgumentError, "Cannot execute #{@@options.cpp}\n" unless File.executable?(file)
        
      143. 
      
        
    143. 
          
          
              else
        
      144. 
      
        
    144. 
          1
          
                if Config::CONFIG["host_os"].downcase =~ /solaris/
        
      145. 
      
        
    145. 
          
          
                  @@options.cpp = "/usr/lib/cpp"
        
      146. 
      
        
    146. 
          
          
                elsif Config::CONFIG["host_os"].downcase =~ /linux/
        
      147. 
      
        
    147. 
          1
          
                  @@options.cpp = "/usr/bin/cpp"
        
      148. 
      
        
    148. 
          
          
                else
        
      149. 
      
        
    149. 
          
          
                  raise RuntimeError, "Unsupported host OS\n"
        
      150. 
      
        
    150. 
          
          
                end
        
      151. 
      
        
    151. 
          
          
              end
        
      152. 
      
        
    152. 
          
          
          
        
      153. 
      
        
    153. 
          
          
              # Check macros. Assign 1 to macros defined only as names.
        
      154. 
      
        
    154. 
          2
          
              @@options.macros.each do |macro|
        
      155. 
      
        
    155. 
          2
          
                macro << "=1" if macro !~ /\=/
        
      156. 
      
        
    156. 
          
          
              end
        
      157. 
      
        
    157. 
          
          
          
        
      158. 
      
        
    158. 
          
          
              # Check that output file name has been given. Set extension to '.py', if none given.
        
      159. 
      
        
    159. 
          2
          
              puts "WARNING: No output file name was given.\n" if @@options.outfile.empty?
        
      160. 
      
        
    160. 
          2
          
              @@options.outfile = @@options.directory + "/" + @@options.args[-1].split(/\//)[-1].slice(0..-5) if @@options.outfile.empty?
        
      161. 
      
        
    161. 
          2
          
              @@options.outfile << ".py" if @@options.outfile.split(/\//)[-1][-3,3] != ".py"
        
      162. 
      
        
    162. 
          
          
              
        
      163. 
      
        
    163. 
          
          
              # Check header files
        
      164. 
      
        
    164. 
          4
          
              @@options.header_files.each {|f| raise ArgumentError, "Cannot open #{f}\n" unless File.readable?(f)}
        
      165. 
      
        
    165. 
          
          
          
        
      166. 
      
        
    166. 
          
          
              # Check include paths
        
      167. 
      
        
    167. 
          2
          
              @@options.include_paths.each {|i| puts "Warning: Non-existent include path #{i}\n" unless File.exists?(i)}
        
      168. 
      
        
    168. 
          
          
            end
        
      169. 
      
        
    169. 
          
          
          
        
      170. 
      
        
    170. 
          
          
          end
        
      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          
          
          
        
      172.

          1

      182.

            end
